CREATE POLICY "Authors can view plagiarism checks on 
their own posts" ON plagiarism_checks
  FOR SELECT                                            
                                  
  USING (                                               
                                  
    EXISTS (                                            
                                  
      SELECT 1 FROM posts                               
                                  
      WHERE posts.id = plagiarism_checks.post_id        
                                  
      AND posts.author_id = (select auth.uid())         
                                  
    )                                                   
                                  
  )
